\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2preprocessing_2__data_8py_source_l02604}02604\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ method\ transforms\ the\ features\ to\ follow\ a\ uniform\ or\ a\ normal}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2preprocessing_2__data_8py_source_l02607}02607\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ (marginal)\ outliers:\ this\ is\ therefore\ a\ robust\ preprocessing\ scheme.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2preprocessing_2__data_8py_source_l02609}02609\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ transformation\ is\ applied\ on\ each\ feature\ independently.\ First\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2preprocessing_2__data_8py_source_l02610}02610\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ estimate\ of\ the\ cumulative\ distribution\ function\ of\ a\ feature\ is}}
